## Page 5

作者介绍

·李春
原里巴巴MySQLDBA团队技术Leader，全程参与
了阿里胶据库架构以Oracle任够题MySQL的过程，
与了分布式中间件Cober设计。现为沃期科技联合创始
人点首席架构师，负度MySQL、基础软件及部分关键
组件的技术选型、风险评钻等。

罗小波
沃难料技高板数据库工程师，主要负责MySQL产品的
量很监控系统、运维管理平台、数据库管理平台的设计数图库支排与售后二线支票，普参与版本家布系统、轻
与编写，热图MySQL体系结构、Innodb存储号撑，喜
好贴研开源接术，多次在公开场合做过线下线上数到库
专题分享，发表过多菌与数望库相关的研究交章。

董红用
沃薄科技MySQLDBA，为多家大型企业做过放障解
决、限构设计、性能优化，例效中国证养、新江农值、
限西农信、邮储银行等，规划并实施了浙江农值互联网
核心金融平台。

<!-- 图源: ./千金良方：MySQL性能优化金字塔法则 (李春  罗小波  等  罗小波  等) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p005_scan.jpg -->

## Page 8

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:22.20pt;color:#c36500">内容简介</span>

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">本书一共分为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">篇：基础篇、案例篇和工具篇。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">基础篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">从理论基础和基本原理层面</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">介绍了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的安装与配置、升级和体系结构，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">information_schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">sys_schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">performance_schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">mysql_schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">复制，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">事务，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">SQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">语句优化及架构设</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">计基础知识。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">案例篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">从硬件和系统、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">架构等方面给出了性能优化的十几个案</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">例，包括：性能测试的基本优化思路和最需要关注的性能指标解释、对日常</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">SQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">语句执行</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">慢的基本定位、避免</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">x86</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">可用性的一般性方法、节能模式会怎样影响性能、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">I/O</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">存储作为数</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">据库最重要的依赖是如何影响数据库性能的、主备复制不一致可能有哪些原因、字符集不</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">一致会造成哪些性能问题、在实际场景中锁的争用是怎样的。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">工具篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">介绍了在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">性能优化过程中需要用到的各种工具，包括：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">dmidecode</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">top</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">dstat</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">等硬件和系统排查工</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">具；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">FIO</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">sysbench</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">HammerDB</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">等压力测试工具；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">mysqldump</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">XtraBackup</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">等备份工具；</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Percona</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">innotop</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Prometheus</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">等监控工具。</span>

## Page 10

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:22.20pt;color:#c36500">推荐序</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:22.20pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">1</span>

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">本书作者李春是阿里巴巴较为早期的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">DBA</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">之一，罗小波和董红禹则都是知数堂的优</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">秀校友。有一次我偶然知道了罗小波的经历，非常令人赞叹，这么努力的人理应获得如此</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">成就。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">第一次注意到罗小波是因为他的投稿文章</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">排序内部原理探秘</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">，该文章真的</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">是从头到尾、从上到下全方位解读了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">内部排序的方方面面。再后来，又关注到罗</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">小波推出</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">PFS</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">sys </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">系列连载文章，更是对其静心深入学习的能力表示钦佩，整个</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">系列文章翔实、细致、到位。另外，董红禹的功底也非常深厚，他对除</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">外的其他</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">数据库也有较多了解。二位同学曾多次被知数堂邀请做公开课分享。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">除此之外，我曾感叹沃趣培养出了不少好工程师，其人才体系肯定有很多可学之处，</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">于是也邀请了李春来知数堂做公开课分享，就是希望能把他们的人才培养机制分享给业</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">界。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">拿到本书书稿，我快速浏览了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">案例篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的全部内容，发现几乎都是精华，里面涉及了</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">相当多的经典案例解析，如果能从这些案例中吸收解决问题的思路，那么相信读者以后若</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">遇到其他问题，基本上都可以解决。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">本书既有涉及体系结构、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">PFS</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">I_S</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、统计信息、复制、锁、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">InnoDB</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">等基础知识的铺</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">垫（其实并不基础），又有众多案例详解，内容丰富、翔实，是难得一见的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">性能</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">优化参考书，建议每位</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">DBA</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">以及从事</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">相关应用开发的读者都读一读。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">最后，说一个段子。我曾经开玩笑地说，大家以后要买书的话，记得先看有没有我给</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">写的推荐序，如果有的话，那就放心买，如果没有的话，那就要谨慎点了。本书我是推荐</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的，所以大家可以放心大胆买。嘿嘿。</span>

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">叶金荣</span>

---

## Page 11

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:22.20pt;color:#c36500">推荐序</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:22.20pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">2</span>

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">小学课本告诉我们，蒸汽机是瓦特看到水壶被水蒸气顶起来以后冥思苦想发明出来</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的。但实际情况其实是，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">17</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">世纪末期，托马斯</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">•</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">纽克曼（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Thomas Newcomen</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">）发明了体积</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">庞大的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">蒸汽机</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">，利用蒸汽的力量把煤矿里的水抽出来，避免了矿井透水、积水的问题。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">1765</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">年，詹姆士</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">•</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">瓦特（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">James Watt</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">）发明了分离式冷凝器，改进了纽克曼蒸汽机，使得蒸</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">汽机的效率提升了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">倍。当然，纽克曼蒸汽机也不是凭空出现的，纽克曼蒸汽机是基于</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Thomas Savery</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">发明的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Savery</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">蒸汽泵的，继续往前追溯，可以追溯到公元</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">世纪古希腊力学</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">家希罗（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Heron of Alexandria</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">）发明的汽转球。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">我并不否认瓦特的贡献，正是有了他对蒸汽机做功效率的改变，才提升了煤炭、钢铁</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的产量，促进了轮船、火车的产生，才有了工业革命。我这里想说的是人们很早就发现了</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">蒸汽做功的理论，但是把它利用起来，把它真正用于我们的生产生活中来提高生产效率的</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">过程是曲折而漫长的，理论和原理的发明是耀眼的明星，工程化实践和持续不断的改进却</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">像星光传到我们的眼睛一样，需要经过漫长的过程，凝聚着很多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">无名</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">科学家和工程师的</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">努力与心血。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">之父</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Monty</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Michael Widenius</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">）在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">1981</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">年写了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的第一行代码以后，在</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">开源的帮助下</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">成长为目前最流行的开源数据库，同样其也凝聚了非常多的开发</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">者、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">DBA</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、工程师的心血。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">2009</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">年，在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">被</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Oracle</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">收购以后，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">47</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">岁的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Monty</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">开发了</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MariaDB</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">分支，到现在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MariaDB</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">也已经</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">10</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">年了，他仍然亲自参与写代码，并且负责大部分</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">代码的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Review</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">工作，我作为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MariaDB</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">基金会的中国成员在跟</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Monty</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">一起</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Review</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">代码时，经</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">常会叹服老爷子对全局的把控能力和对细节的严谨态度。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">2016</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">年当</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Monty</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">在阿里巴巴交流</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">分享时，我问</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Monty</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">你怎么看阿里巴巴在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">方面的能力以及贡献？</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">他说：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">你贡</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">献的多源复制和闪回功能，对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MariaDB</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">很有用，因此我觉得你和你的团队是很有能力的，</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">也希望能获得更多的来自各大厂商和社区的贡献。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">之所以能成为现在最流行的开源数据库，这跟它的开放性、包容性是分不开</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的。它的入门门槛低到用一条命令就能把</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">安装起来，你能在程序开发的入门资料</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">中很容易就找到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的配套使用教程，你可以不用付任何费用就能在自己的环境中部</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">署起来对外承载业务。我之前提交的代码补足了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">在某些方面的功能，是对它的贡</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">献；苏普验证测试时发现</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL 5.6</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的半同步</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Bug</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">汇报给社区，是对它的贡献；李春他们</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">撰写</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">书籍，也是对它的贡献。我和阿里巴巴的其他同事翻译《高性能</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">》时</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">就体会到了出版一本书的艰辛，所以看到《千金良方：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">性能优化金字塔法则》这</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">本沉甸甸的书时，完全能感受到三位作者在写书时的痛苦与艰辛。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">5.5</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">版本开始引入</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">performance_schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">，从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">5.6</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">版本开始把默认值设置为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">on</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">我个人认为从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">5.7</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">版本（对应</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MariaDB </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">10.1</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">）开始它才真正成熟起来。从某种程度上说，</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">performance_schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的引入对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">来说可以类比于瓦特发明分离式冷凝器改进蒸汽机，</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">使得开发人员或者</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">DBA</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的性能损耗能准确定位到源码层级，对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的管控也</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">可以更加精细化。这本书是我了解到的第一本体系化介绍</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">performance_schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的书，对</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">性能优化有兴趣的读者可以参阅。</span>

---

## Page 12

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">另外，本书</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">案例篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">也是我见过的相对比较系统化介绍性能优化方面的内容，从服务</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">器、操作系统、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">SQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">和锁方面整体梳理了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">性能优化的方方面面，相关案</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">例都具有代表性，很值得参考和验证，也希望读者能参考案例来验证和测试，并举一反</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">三，结合自己环境的实际场景构建起性能改进的方法论。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">蒸汽机的改进不是一蹴而就的，性能的改进也是贯穿整个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">发展史的，就像瓦</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">特改进蒸汽机引发了工业革命一样，我希望本书的出版能进一步促进大家对</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL/MariaDB</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">性能优化的关注，能为最流行的开源数据库</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL/MariaDB</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">大厦添砖加</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">瓦。</span>

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">彭立勋</span>

---

## Page 13

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:22.20pt;color:#c36500">推荐序</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:22.20pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">3</span>

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">我先说一个笑话。这个笑话是我从万维钢的专栏里看到的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">三个逻辑学家走进酒吧，酒保问他们，三位都喝啤酒吗？</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">第一个逻辑学家说，我不知道。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">第二个逻辑学家说，我不知道。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">第三个逻辑学家说，是的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">这个笑话有点冷，需要用一点逻辑才能欣赏。要想否定</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">三人都喝啤酒</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">，只要有一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">人知道自己不喝就行了。前两个逻辑学家说不知道，就说明他们自己是想喝的，只是不知</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">道别人喝不喝。而第三个人一看前两个人都说不知道，那就说明这两个人肯定都是要喝</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的，而他自己也想喝啤酒，所以他就可以判断三人都想喝啤酒。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">他们的回答有点怪，但是非常准确。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">为什么要讲这个故事呢？因为我的这三位同事李春、罗小波、董红禹在我头脑里的画</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">像都是非常认真和讲究逻辑的人。这种认真和严谨，你在书中的每一页都能感受到。相信</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">通过这本书的系统性训练，你也能感受到这种思维方式的美，最终也能获得这种思维方</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">式。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">授人以鱼，不如授之以渔。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">具备优秀的思维能力才是在未来可以迁移的能力，如果</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">只是学习一些命令，则很快会过时，思维能力和学习能力的提升才是不会变的东西。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">说回到这本书。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">对这本书的起心动念，我是有功劳的，所以李春邀请我来写序，也就很痛快地答应</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">一年前我们在想，我们有着业界一流的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">团队，为什么不能将这些知识和经验</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">以一种更容易传播的方式贡献给大家呢？</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">沿着这个思路，想到了两种载体，一种是产品，这也是沃趣一直在做的，未来也会一</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">直持续做；一种是书籍，书籍其实也是一种产品，因为它也是标准化的、极容易复制的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">因此，团队中在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">技术上颇有追求和建树的几个人碰头一聊，大家一拍即合。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">起心动念容易，甚至一度让我们很兴奋，但是落地难，尤其是在做了管理者带了团队</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">之后，更能意识到这一点，提建议（起心动念）是没有成本的，但是具体做这件事、落地</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">这件事的人是需要忍受寂寞、付出巨大努力的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">我在他们的写作群里，见证了写书过程中的所有艰辛。好在一年的时间，坚持下来</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">了，成果就是各位手里拿到的这本书。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">学知识，如果说有捷径，那就是选择几本靠谱的、高质量的书籍，站在巨人的肩膀</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">上，这是高起点和借势。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">这本书可以让你体验到原有知识从破碎到重建的过程，只有能打破你现有认知的书籍</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">才是好书籍，打破之后，如果你能够重建起基于新认知的知识大厦，你就重生了。对于认</span>

## Page 14

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">知是如此，对于心智、对于各种成长莫不如此。格物致知，相信通过努力学习这本书，会</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">带给你底层认知的提升。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">在这里也要恭喜我的几位同事：李春、罗小波、董红禹，写书是大多数技术人员的梦</span>

---

## Page 15

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:22.20pt;color:#c36500">前言</span>

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">性能问题</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">这个世界是由问题组成的，理想的状态和实际状态之间的差异造成了问题。国家领导</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">解决人民生活幸福的大问题，公司的总经理解决盈利的问题，而本书只想解决</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">数</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">据库性能这么一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">小问题</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">从某种程度来说，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">数据库性能优化的问题是一个并行的问题，归根结底是锁</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">和资源争用的问题。举个例子：假设你要开一个餐饮店，你需要取好店名，到工商局领取</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">开业登记注册证书，到卫生防疫站申请卫生许可，到物价局进行物价审核，如果要卖酒，</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">则需要到工商部门办理酒类经营许可证，到税务局办理税务登记，到银行开户，还需要找</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">厨师、找洗碗工、找采购人员、找门面、协调店面转让、进行店面装修、做广告牌，等</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">等。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">如果想尽快把餐饮店开起来，就需要同时做更多的事情，就像计算机一样，并行地去</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">做更多的事情。但是当你真正去做这些事情的时候，会发现：</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">•</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">总有一两件事情耗费的时间特别长，会最大程度地影响餐饮店什么时候能开起来。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">比如找到合适的店面或者合适的厨师。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">•</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">有些事情是相互依赖的，一件事情必须依赖于另一件事情的完成。比如工商登记就</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">取决于你要准备好店名，店面装修依赖于门面已经租好了，等等。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">•</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">有些事情特别重要，它决定了这个餐饮店是否能长期经营下去。例如厨师做的菜是</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">否足够好、足够快，运营的成本是否足够低而能产生足够的利润支撑餐饮店继续运营。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">其实性能优化要做的就是以下事情：</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">•</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">了解基本原理。找到事情的因果关系和依赖关系，让尽量不相关的事情能并行做起</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">来。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">•</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">要事第一。找到当前最重要、最需要优化的地方，投入时间和精力，不断去改进</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">它、优化它。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">•</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">切中要害。找到耗费时间最长的地方，想方设法缩短它的时间。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">本书的作者尝试通过上述方法论来找到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">性能优化的办法并呈现给读者。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">数据库的性能提升</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">从计算机出现的第一天起，性能作为鞭策者就不断地促进计算机及系统的演进。从最</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">开始的人工输入命令等待计算机执行，到利用批处理任务提升利用率，再到通过多进程和</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">多线程并发来进一步提升效率，性能其实一直是计算机工程师想要努力去解决和改善的重</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">要难题。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">上面说的都是对已有系统的性能优化，数据库的性能优化其实可以在做设计之前就开</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">始了。</span>

---

## Page 16

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">数据库的性能优化首先是计算机系统的优化。数据库程序是运行在计算机系统上的应</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">用程序，需要先优化的就是计算机系统。也就是说，让硬件尽量均衡，操作系统充分发挥</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">硬件的全部性能，而数据库充分利用操作系统和文件系统提供的便利发挥全部性能，而且</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">避免资源的相互竞争。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">数据库的性能优化其次是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">SQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">语句的优化。上层应用都通过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">SQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">语句与数据库打交</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">道，一条</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">SQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">语句为了获取数据可以有几十甚至上百种执行计划，数据库会通过优化器选</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">择更优的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">SQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">执行计划，但是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">在执行计划上远远落后于商业数据库，甚至在一些</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">方面相比</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">PostgreSQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">也差很多，那么怎么写出正确的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">SQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">语句，避免</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">选择错误的</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">执行计划，以及怎样通过增加索引、设置参数让</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的执行计划更优，这就是优化</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">SQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">语句需要关心的事情。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">最后，数据库的性能优化最有效的是架构的优化。对于读多写少的应用程序，可以设</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">计为读写分离，把允许延迟的读请求主动分发到备库；对于秒杀型的业务，可以先在内存</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">型</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">key-value</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">存储系统筛选再发往数据库持久化，避免对数据库的冲击；对于汇总、聚合类</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的应用，可以采用列式存储引擎或者专门的大数据平台；对于监控类的应用，可以采用时</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">序数据库，等等。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">以上三种优化思路贯穿本书，这也是本书名为《千金良方：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">性能优化金字塔</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">法则》的缘由。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">机械思维和大数据思维</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">看过吴军博士《智能时代：大数据与智能革命重新定义未来》的人可能会对本书嗤之</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">以鼻，本书的性能优化方法论还是工业革命时代的机械思维，简而言之，就是寻找因果关</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">系，大胆假设，小心求证。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">现在都是信息时代了，了解过信息论没有？知道香农第一定</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">律和第二定律吗？解决问题需要用大数据思维！</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">笔者有两点理由使用机械思维来介绍数据库性能优化：</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">）大数据时代需要的数据量大、多纬度和完备性，目前对数据库的性能优化和性</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">能诊断，笔者掌握的案例和相关信息远远达不到大数据的要求。我们可以期待亚马逊、阿</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">里云或者腾讯云等厂商或者专业的数据库公司（如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Oracle</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MariaDB</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">等）来有针对性地做</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">一些大数据数据库性能优化的尝试。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">）大数据的成本很高。目前我们遇到的大部分性能问题其实用因果关系和假设</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">→</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">推导</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">→</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">再假设</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">→</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">再推导的方法就可以解决，不需要用到大数据、人工智能这样的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">大杀</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">器</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">内容介绍</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的火热程度有目共睹，如果需要了解</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的安装、启动、配置等基础知</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">识，市面上相关的书籍已是汗牛充栋。本书则尽量深入细致地介绍</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的基本原理，</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">以及性能优化的实际案例。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">基本原理很枯燥，就像课堂上老师介绍数学定理和公式推导一样，有人可能会质疑，</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">小学都在进行素质教育了，你这本书里怎么还有那么多基本原理的介绍？对于工作了两三</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">年的技术人员来说，在实践上已经有了比较多的积累，解决过很多问题</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">——</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">可能通过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">sys</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">查询事务锁等待解决了系统的并发问题，通过设置</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">ulimit -n </span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">扩大进程文件句柄数解</span>

---

## Page 17

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">决了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的进程限制问题，通过设计读写分离架构扩展了应用的读性能线性扩展问</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">题。但是作为求知欲强的技术人员，我们急切地希望知其所以然，了解</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">到底是怎</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">么设计的，以及为什么这样设计，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">sys schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">到底还有哪些可以帮助我们分析解决问题的</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">存储过程，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">系统的资源限制除了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">ulimit</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">还有哪些，读写分离架构适应的场景有哪些，</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">什么时候建议用分库分表，等等。如果你也跟我们一样，你应该阅读本书。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">本书一共分为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">篇：基础篇、案例篇和工具篇。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">信息论认为消除一件事情的不确定性就是获取足够多的信息。我们认为任何优化都可</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">以从了解它的基本原理和设计思路开始。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">基础篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">从理论基础和基本原理层面介绍了</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的安装与配置、升级和体系结构，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">information_schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">sys_schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">performance_schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">mysql_schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">复制，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">事务，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">SQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">语句优化及架构设</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">计基础知识。希望读者通过对这些内容的学习，能够深入细致地了解</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">各方面的基</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">础知识。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">计算机是一种实验的科学，性能优化是实战的艺术。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">案例篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">从硬件和系统、</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">架构等方面给出了性能优化的十几个案例，包括：性能测试的基本优化思路和最</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">需要关注的性能指标解释、对日常</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">SQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">语句执行慢的基本定位、避免</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">x86</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">可用性的一般性</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">方法、节能模式会怎样影响性能、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">I/O</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">存储作为数据库最重要的依赖是如何影响数据库性</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">能的、主备复制不一致可能有哪些原因、字符集不一致会造成哪些性能问题、在实际场景</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">中锁的争用是怎样的。希望读者通过这些案例，可以深入细致地理解</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">基础篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">中的各种概</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">念，融会贯通，对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">有一个全面的、系统的掌握。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">工欲善其事，必先利其器。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">我们日常需要借助一些工具来做性能优化。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">工具篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">介</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">绍了在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">性能优化过程中需要用到的各种工具，包括：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">dmidecode</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">top</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">dstat</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">等硬件</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">和系统排查工具；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">FIO</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">sysbench</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">HammerDB</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">等压力测试工具；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">mysqldump</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">XtraBackup</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">等备份工具；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Percona</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">innotop</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">Prometheus</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">等监控工具。希望读者可以借助更多自动化的</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">方式去验证和评估性能优化解决方案，提升性能。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">读者对象</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">初学者。建议按照顺序从本书的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">基础篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">开始阅读。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">基础篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">介绍了从</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">安装部署、基础配置到性能诊断等日常工作需要了解的内容。在熟悉了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的基本概</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">念和大致原理以后，在阅读</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">案例篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">时，对问题的定义和解决方案才能理解得更加透彻。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">最后在阅读</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">工具篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">时，也可以学习到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL DBA</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">日常工作所需工具的使用方法和应用</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">场景。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">）专门从事</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">工作</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">1~3</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">年的开发人员和运维人员。对于有一些</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">开发和</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">运维经验的人员，建议先跳过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">基础篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">，直接从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">案例篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">开始阅读。在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">案例篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">中了解了</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">具体的问题现象、故障处理的过程和方法以后，联系案例中对应的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">基础篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">工具篇</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">知</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">识进行阅读，这样能帮助你把很多知识点串联起来，由点到面形成更为全面的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">知</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">识体系。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">）资深的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">DBA</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">。本书可以作为案头书，在解决问题时，如果记不清某些</span>

## Page 41

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:24.00pt;color:#c36500">基础篇</span>

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">基础篇的内容设计，旨在为大家普及一些在性能优化过程中可能使用到的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">基</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">础知识。为了方便大家对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的体系结构和组件有一个整体认识，首先，完整介绍</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的安装、升级和整个体系组成结构，并介绍在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">运行过程中所有后台线程的</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">作用；其次，由于在性能优化过程中需要依赖与表</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">/</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">索引相关的统计信息、事务锁和表级</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">锁相关信息、在语句执行过程中的一些等待事件信息等，我们用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">14</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">个章节重点介绍</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">个系统库：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">information_schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">mysql</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">performance_schema</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">sys</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">，通过这些</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">系统库中记录的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的状态和性能数据，读者可以更精确地定位问题的根源，甚至定</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">位到源码的某一行；最后，除在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">复制、事务和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">SQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">优化章节介绍</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">自身的优</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">化基础以外，还通过读写扩展的架构优化，抛砖引玉，希望引起读者对架构优化的思考。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">相信大家通过阅读基础篇的内容一定会有所收获。</span>

## Page 42

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:22.20pt;color:#c36500">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:22.20pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">1</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:22.20pt;color:#c36500">章　</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:22.20pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:22.20pt;color:#c36500">初始化安装、简单安全加固</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">从这里开始，我们开启了本书的第一个章节。为了方便后续演示，以及照顾一些基础较为薄弱的读者，我</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">们决定在本书中加入安装</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">的章节，请大家准备好一台</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">服务器，跟随本章内容进行同步操作。</span>

## Page 44

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">的程序访问路径</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">/usr/local/mysql</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">下，并把</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">/usr/local/mysql/bin/</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">添加到系统环境变量中，以便</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">mysql</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">相关命令时不需要输入绝对路径。</span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">1.2.6</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:16.80pt;color:#c36500">　配置</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">my.cnf</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:16.80pt;color:#c36500">文件参数</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">把样例配置文件复制到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">/home/mysql/conf</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">目录下，并设置好相关路径系统参数：</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">socket</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">pid-file</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">datadir</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">tmpdir</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">log-error</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">slow_query_log_file</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">log-bin</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">relay-log</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">innodb_data_ home_dir</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">innodb_log_group_home_dir</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">innodb_undo_directory</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">。</span>

## Page 45

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">1.2.7</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:16.80pt;color:#c36500">　初始化</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">MySQL</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">mysql_install_db</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">命令初始化</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">数据字典库、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">ibdata1</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">log_file*</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">等文件。</span>

## Page 46

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">提示：在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL 5.7</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">版本中删除了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">mysql_install_db</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">脚本，直接使用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">bin/mysqld</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">命令进程初始化，初始化有</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">两个选项。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">•</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">　</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">--initialize</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">：使用该选项初始化时会在错误日志中写一个随机的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">root</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">密码，初始化</span>

![](./千金良方：MySQL性能优化金字塔法则 (李春  罗小波  等  罗小波  等) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p046_img01.jpg)

---

## Page 47

<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">完成之后在错误日志中搜索</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">password</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">，紧跟其后的一串字符串就是这个随机密码（例</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">如，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">“A temporary password is generated for root@localhost: XRER&lt;:les9p?”</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">这段文字中的粗</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">体字部分就是随机密码），初始化完成并启动</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">mysqld</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">之后，初次登录需要使用这个随机密</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">码。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">•</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">　</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">--initialize-insecure</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">：使用该选项初始化时不会产生随机密码，而是像</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL 5.7</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">之</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">前的版本一样，初始化完成之后，第一次登录数据库使用空的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">root</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">密码。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">示例：</span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">1.2.8</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:16.80pt;color:#c36500">　启动</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">MySQL</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">将</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">mysql.server</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">文件复制到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">/etc/init.d/</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">目录下，命名为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">mysqld</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">程序，并使用这个脚本启</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">动和停止</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">。</span>

![](./千金良方：MySQL性能优化金字塔法则 (李春  罗小波  等  罗小波  等) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p047_img01.jpg)

-initialize

## Page 48

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:19.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">1.3</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:19.80pt;color:#c36500">　简单安全加固</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">1.3.1</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:16.80pt;color:#c36500">　登录</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">MySQL</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL 5.6.x</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">初始化完成并启动之后，可以使用免密码的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">root</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">用户登录</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">，同时</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">查看</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">版本和登录用户是否是想要的结果。</span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">1.3.2</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:16.80pt;color:#c36500">　删除非</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">root</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:16.80pt;color:#c36500">或非</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">localhost</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:16.80pt;color:#c36500">的用户并修改</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">root</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:16.80pt;color:#c36500">密码</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">在默认情况下，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">初始化完成之后，创建了一些默认用户：匿名用户、允许</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">127.0.0.1</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">localhost</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">登录的非</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">root</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">用户，建议删除这些无用且可能给数据库带来安全风险的</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">用户。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">提示：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">安全加固也可以使用命令行工具</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">mysql_secure_installation</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">，根据提示一步一步执行即可。</span>

![](./千金良方：MySQL性能优化金字塔法则 (李春  罗小波  等  罗小波  等) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p048_img01.jpg)

## Page 50

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">1.3.3</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:16.80pt;color:#c36500">　删除</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">test</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:16.80pt;color:#c36500">库，清理</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:16.80pt;font-weight:bold;color:#c36500">mysql.db</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:16.80pt;color:#c36500">表</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">在默认情况下，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL 5.6.x</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">初始化安装之后会生成一个测试用途的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">test</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">库，这个库在</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">生产环境中一般不需要使用，如果确定不使用，请删除。</span>
<span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">在默认情况下，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL 5.6.x</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">初始化完成</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'NSimSun';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">之后，
